WHERE ARE ALL THE REEL-ENTHUSIASTS?

📍Make 45-60 seconds reel and send it attached in the registration link, 
📍The reel should highlight ‘Patriotism’ and you can showcase any art form including dancing, singing, poetry etc. 
The stage is all yours!!! 🥳
What are the perks for participation?
 ✔️Selected reels will get featured on the official page of Alankrit
✔️Shout-out to winners
✔️ Participation certificates
So what is taking you so long to miss out on this amazing opportunity ? 
Compete and win! 
Let's celebrate 26th January with zeal and enthusiasm.

24/01/2023, 12:04 pm - +91 89602 13088: सस्वर (ज़िंदगी हो राष्ट्र गीत)💐

विषय: गणतंत्र भारत (Republic india)

काव्यांजलि साहित्यिक समिति, गणतंत्र दिवस के इस शुभ अवसर पर वीडियो के माध्यम से काव्य पाठ प्रतियोगिता का अयोजन करवा रही है। प्रतिभागियों को एक स्वरचित कविता सुनाते हुए अपना एक वीडियो रिकॉर्ड करना होगा, सर्वश्रेष्ठ 3 वीडियो काव्यांजलि के सोशल मीडिया पर पोस्ट किए जाएंगे।

नियम और विनियम:-
•कविता स्वरचित होनी चाहिए।
•वीडियो की न्यूनतम सीमा 1 मिनट व अधिकतम सीमा 2 मिनट होगी। 
•स्वरचित कविता राजनैतिक एवं धार्मिक भावनाओं को क्षति पहुंचाने वाली ना हो।
•विजेता का चयन सभी उल्लिखित नियमों के आधार पर किया जाएगा।
•कविता का माध्यम हिन्दी एवं अंग्रेज़ी हो सकता है।

संपर्क- 9760669284
कुँवर सूर्य प्रताप सिंह (उपाध्यक्ष काव्यांजलि)
24/01/2023, 12:04 pm - +91 89602 13088: <Media omitted>
24/01/2023, 12:05 pm - +91 89602 13088: <Media omitted>
24/01/2023, 12:05 pm - +91 89602 13088: 🇮🇳तिरंगा लहरायेंगे,
भक्ति गीत गुनगुनाएंगे,
वादा करो इस देश को,
दुनिया का सबसे प्यारा देश बनायेंगे।🇮🇳

सत्य ही कहा गया है कि संविधान की प्रस्तावना (Preamble) ही उसकी आत्मा है। तो इस गणतंत्र दिवस काव्यांजलि साहित्यिक समिति आप सभी के लिए लेकर आई है
 ✨ अभिव्यंजना ✨
एक ऐसी प्रतियोगिता जिसके अंतर्गत आप सभी को भारत के संविधान की प्रस्तावना को अपनी आवाज़ में रिकॉर्ड करना होगा। इसका माध्यम हिंदी होगा।

मूल्यांकन के नियम -

1. आप सभी को पोस्टर में दी गई प्रस्तावना को अपनी वाणी में रिकॉर्ड करना है।

2. इसकी कोई समय सीमा नहीं है।

3. आप सभी से निवेदन है कि अपनी audio को voice cancellation करके ही अपलोड करें।

4. आप बैकग्राउंड म्यूजिक का उपयोग कर सकते हैं।

5. मूल्यांकन के मानदंड होंगे 
 शब्दों की शुद्धता, स्वर का उतार चढ़ाव एवं वाणी की स्पष्टता।

✨ विजेता की ऑडियो को काव्यांजलि साहित्यिक समिति के Spotify पेज पर डाला जायेगा। सभी प्रतिभागियों को सर्टिफिकेट प्रदान किए जाएंगे। ✨

उम्मीद है आप सभी इस प्रतियोगिता में बढ़ चढ़कर हिस्सा लेंगे व देश हित में किए गए इस प्रयास को सफल बनाने में सहयोग करेंगे।

पंजिकरण करें -
https://forms.gle/YTki4uLYrBCa9Zjs5
(Or scan the QR code)

कृतिका- An Online E-poster making competition 🌅

In this competition, you have to make a digital poster using any application(Canva,Photoshop etc) on theme of “बसंत पंचमी”.🌻
It can be representing a wish(Happy Vasant Panchami) or anything that you can create with the idea of the theme.

Rules include:

1. There is no language barrier. The poster can be in Hindi or English.
2. The size of the poster will be a square post with dimensions 1080px by 1080px at a 1:1 aspect ratio.
3. Poster shouldn’t hurt the sentiments of any culture,religion etc. They should not be politically related.
4. Plagiarism to be avoided at all costs. Only original work will be acknowledged.
5. Judging criteria will be based upon:
 •Creativity 
 •Originality 
 •Aesthetics

Hello Everyone!

We, *The Designnovation Hub*, in collaboration with *ACM AND ACM-W* are excited to announce an upcoming interactive session *“MENTOR MIX”* where you can learn from the experiences and insights of some high-achieving 3rd and 4th year *students having an experience* in companies like *ATLASSIAN, MICROSOFT, ADOBE, AMAZON, ZSCALER, FLIPKART, LINKEDIN, and have done research at IIIT delhi.*

The session will be an open forum where you can engage in a dialogue with some of the most successful students in our program. They will share their insights on *topics* such as: 
✅Placement preparations and extracurriculars
✅Different projects and technical skills
✅Resume building
✅Online assessments
✅Research and academia
✅Application processes
✅Cold emailing
✅Pursuing masters abroad
✅Time Management
✅Navigating social life along with academics

The event aims at providing students of the first and second year with some tips. The learnings of the speakers would help the audience prepare in the best way for their careers with the proper guidance and support. 

Whether you are just starting out or have been studying for a while, you are sure to benefit from this session.

Please mark your calendars for the event, which will take place on 📆*8th April 2023* at ⏰*10 AM* and *do register yourself!*

Hello Everyone!

We, *The Designnovation Hub*, in collaboration with *Debsoc*(The Offical Debating Society of Graphic Era University), are excited to announce an upcoming event *“GROUP DISCUSSION”* where you have the opportunity to both learn skills required to ace a group discussion through a *GD Workshop* and to put them to the test by participating in a *GD competition*. 

The two-day event aims at:
✅Provide technical knowledge of GDs.
✅ Help in Placement training.
✅Teach students social and public speaking skills.  
✅To enhance the listening skills and confidence of students.

The two-day event will help you with the necessary skills and knowledge required to qualify for Group Discussions during placements and you get to put those skills to the test by participating and competing against your batchmates.

*The Workshop will be conducted by the PDP Department*

Please mark your calendars for the two-day event, which will take place on 
🟩 *22nd May from 2pm* onwards(Workshop)
🟩 *23rd May from 12pm* onwards(Competition ), 

and do register yourself!

🏫Venue for the event: Seminar hall,CSIT Block
Reporting time: 
1:45 PM on 18th May and 
12:00 PM on 19th May.

📜Certificate of attendance will be provided & Exciting Prices for the Best Speakers’ 

🍀Follow us on Instagram: @tdhgeu & @debsoc_geu

We are looking forward to see you there! 🌻

It is our utmost pleasure to provide you a platform where you can discover your oratory skills. A platform where you can voice your opinion on the question that has troubled thinkers since years.

*“Societal and Ethical Implications of Advancing Artificial Intelligence a threat to humanity ?"*

Mode of Speaking: *Bilingual* (either English only or Hindi only) 
Individual Speaker Time: 2.5 mins

28/06/2023, 12:06 am - Shreya: //KMP
#include <iostream>
using namespace std;
#include<vector>
vector<int> lps_array(string pattern,int m) {
    int len=0,i=1;
    vector<int> lps(m,0);
    while(i<m)  {
        if(pattern[i]==pattern[len]){
            len++;
            lps[i]=len;
            i++;
        }
        else{
            if(len!=0)  {
                len=lps[len-1];
            }
            else    {
                lps[i]=0;
                i++;
            }
        }
    }
    for(int i=0;i<lps.size();i++)
        cout<<lps[i]<<" ";
    cout<<endl;
    return lps;
}
int match_string(string text, int n, string pattern, int m){
    vector<int> lps=lps_array(pattern,m);
    int index=0,i=0,j=0;
    while(i<n)  {
        if(text[i]==pattern[j]){
            i++;
            j++;
        }
        if(j==m)
            j=lps[j-1];
        else{
            if(j!=0)    
                j=lps[j-1];
            else
                i++;
        }
    }
    index=i-m+1;
    return index;
}
int main()
{
    string text,pattern;
    cout<<"TEXT: ";
    getline(cin,text);
    cout<<"PATTERN: ";
    getline(cin,pattern);
    int n,m;
    n=text.length();
    m=pattern.length();
    cout<<n<<m<<endl;
    cout<<"Pattern matched at index: "<<match_string(text,n,pattern,m);
    return 0;
}

int main(){

Atlassian is a software development company responsible for building productivity & collaboration tools such as Jira, Confluence, Trello, and Bitbucket to help teams across the world become nimble, creative, and aligned. As part of the Women in Tech 3.0 program, we aim at hiring students in Software Engineering - Summer Intern roles. This is a wonderful opportunity for students to intern at an organization rated amongst the “Top 10 Places to Work in India” by Great Place to Work.

Eligibility Criteria:

Women students pursuing B.E/B.Tech degrees in the following branches: CSE, EE, IT, ECE, Mathematics and computing. 

A minimum CGPA of 7 or above is required.

Year of passing - 2025

4-year engineering program students only. 

Applicants must not have any current/active backlogs.

If a student has been part of Atlassian’s hiring process in the last 6 months, which includes either coding tests or interviews, please note that they are not eligible to participate in this event


Summer Internship Details:

Internship Timelines - Between May - July 2024 - 8 weeks internship (based on academic schedule)

Monthly Stipend - INR 1,30,000/- 

Students will be eligible to receive a pre-placement offer based on their internship performance

#define e 0.0001
double calc (double x)
{
	return x*x*x-4*x+1;
}
void main()
{
int i=1;
double f=0,lower=0,upper=0;
double a,b,mid=0;
int count=0;
scanf("%lf%lf",&a,&b);
	if (calc(a)*calc(b)<0)
	{
		do
		{
			count++;
			mid=(a+b)/2;
			if (calc(a)<0 && calc(mid)<0 && calc(b)>0)
				a=mid;
			else if (calc(a)<0 && calc(mid)>0 && calc(b)>0)
				b=mid;
			else if (calc(a)>0 && calc(mid)<0 && calc(b)<0)
				b=mid;
			else
				a=mid;

		}while (fabs(calc(a)-calc(b))>e);

	printf ("Loop ran %d times",count);

04/09/2023, 2:08 pm - +91 80573 41977: /*wap in c create pipe, which forks a child process and demostrate communication between parent and child process*/

#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <unistd.h>
#include <sys/types.h>
#include <sys/wait.h>

int main() {
  int pipefds[2];
    char *msg = "hello";
    char buffer[6];


  if (pipe(pipefds) == -1) {
        perror("Pipe creation failed");
        
    }
 
  pid_t pid = fork();
 
  if(pid == 0) { 
    msg = "hello"; 
    close(pipefds[0]); 
    write(pipefds[1], msg, 6); 
 
    printf("sending msg to parent from child\n");
    sleep(2); 
    
  }
 
  if(pid > 0) { 
    wait(NULL); 
    close(pipefds[1]); 
    read(pipefds[0], buffer, 5); 
    close(pipefds[0]); 
 
    printf("msg recived by parent: '%s'\n", buffer);
  }
 
  return 0;
}

We are excited to announce that the IEI Student Chapter Club for Computer Science and Engineering (CSE) is now opening its membership drive!

*Why Join Us? 
The IEI Student Chapter Club for CSE is a vibrant community of tech enthusiasts, innovators, and problem solvers. Here's what sets us apart:

Diverse Learning Opportunities: Our club offers a diverse range of activities, including hands-on workshops, seminars by industry experts, coding challenges, and tech talks, all aimed at enriching your technical knowledge and skills.

Innovation at the Core: We encourage innovation and creativity. Our club provides a platform for you to collaborate on innovative projects and participate in hackathons where you can apply your skills to real-world problems.

Networking and Connections: Connect with like-minded peers, renowned faculty members, and industry professionals. Building these connections can open doors to exciting career opportunities and collaborations.

Skill Enhancement: Whether you're looking to enhance your coding skills, develop project management expertise, or improve your problem-solving abilities, our club is here to help you grow.

25/09/2023, 10:02 pm - +91 98823 47173: CREATE TABLE STUDENT (
    regno VARCHAR(20) PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(50),
    address VARCHAR(100),
    bdate DATE,
    Phone_no CHAR(10)
);

CREATE TABLE COURSE (
    courseno INT PRIMARY KEY,
    cname VARCHAR(50),
    dept VARCHAR(20)
);

CREATE TABLE ENROLL (
    regno VARCHAR(20),
    courseno INT,
    sem INT,
    marks INT,
    PRIMARY KEY (regno, courseno, sem),
    FOREIGN KEY (regno) REFERENCES STUDENT(regno),
    FOREIGN KEY (courseno) REFERENCES COURSE(courseno)
);

CREATE TABLE BOOK_ADOPTION (
    courseno INT,
    sem INT,
    book_isbn INT,
    PRIMARY KEY (courseno, sem),
    FOREIGN KEY (courseno) REFERENCES COURSE(courseno),
    FOREIGN KEY (book_isbn) REFERENCES TEXT(book_isbn)
);

CREATE TABLE TEXT (
    book_isbn INT PRIMARY KEY,
    book_title VARCHAR(100),
    publisher VARCHAR(50),
    author VARCHAR(50)
);
